<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一次，佛告訴比丘們說，如果眾生對於眼耳鼻舌身、色聲香味觸等色蘊有愛著、有喜貪的話，就相當於是愛著於苦。世間人往往不知道這是愛著於苦，於是，耗費了一輩子，最終所做的多是在追求苦惱，只要無法看清真相而繼續愛喜於苦，就無法解脫諸苦。同理，受、想、行、識也是如此。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　反過來說，倘若比丘對於色能不貪愛喜著，就相當於是不喜愛追求諸苦；如果能有智慧的看穿它，不喜著於苦的，也就能解脫於苦。同樣的受想行識也是如此，都不應該對它們生起喜貪與愛著。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　比丘們聽聞佛這樣的開示後，對其中的法理感到歡喜，因此能依教奉行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是與論文相關的《雜阿含經》第十經。另外，結集時為了方便記憶、背誦，在每十部經之後，便有一個攝頌。而「陰相應」第1至10經的攝頌，也以標楷體表示於下：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第10頁：陰相應第1～10經攝頌；累計經數10經；大正藏（7）經<br />
　無常及苦、空，非我、正思惟，無知等四種，及於色喜樂。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是列於十部經之後的攝頌，其中總攝了前十經的內容：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從第1經開始說的是無常，當觀色無常；第2至4經則說：如觀無常，也要觀苦、空、非我；第5經再說到正思惟，比丘於色當正思惟，觀色無常如實知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第6至9經提到了無知（不知、不明、不斷、不離欲）等四種法，只是字句上有些微差異，但主題都是無知；第6經是說，若不知、不明、不斷、不離欲，則不能斷苦；第7經則說心不解脫者，則不能越生老病死怖；第8經說心不解脫，則不能斷苦；第9經說心不解脫者，則不能越生老病死怖；將第6至9經歸成攝頌中的第二句，就是「無知等四種」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　最後，第10經，要對應攝頌中的第三句「及於色喜樂」，經中佛點出了於五蘊愛喜者，即是愛喜於苦，一旦愛著諸苦，便無法解脫諸苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上幾個字，就簡明扼要的收攝了十部經的要義。這幾部經都是很相關的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸七、無常等定2　子一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科無常等定，說明「行擇攝」第一個別頌（界攝）中，第二句「愚相無常等定界」的「無常等定」，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，於諸行中有四決定。一、無常決定，二、苦決定，三、空決定，四、無我決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，在遷流不息的五蘊當中，有四個特性是決定的，一、決定是無常的；二、決定是苦的，絕對不是樂的；三、決定是空的，五蘊之中並沒有一個實我住在那裡，無論即蘊或離蘊都是沒有我的。四、無我決定，有為法的五蘊本身是因緣所生，是不自在的，不是自己所能控制的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、隨釋3　丑一、由三相4　寅一、無常決定2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分三科；第一科由三相，由三相說明諸行是無常、苦、空、無我的，又分四科；第一科無常決定，解釋五蘊決定是無常的，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何諸行無常決定？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為何有為的色受想行識決定是無常的？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋5　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分五科；第一科標，標出三相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由三種相，當知過去、未來諸行尚定無常，何況現在。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由三種相貌，應當知道過去、未來的有為諸行決定是無常的，何況是現在的有為法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為三？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪三種相貌？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列舉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂先無而有故，先有而無故，起盡相應故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由一、先無而有故（未來的五蘊），二、先有而無故（過去的五蘊），三、起盡相應故（現在的五蘊），來說明三世五蘊諸行決定是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這就時間上而言，站在現在的角度去思考未來與過去：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、先無而有是約未來諸行說，未來諸行還沒有來，所以是無，但來到現在是有的，所以是先無而有。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、先有而無是約過去諸行說，過去五蘊諸行本來是有的，但現在滅盡消逝，所以是先有而無。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、起盡相應，則是約現在諸行說，是剎那生起又剎那盡滅，所以是起盡相應。由三世證明諸行決定是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6440"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、釋3　巳一、先無而有2　午一、反顯</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科先無而有，解釋未來的五蘊先無而有，又分二科；第一科反顯，用逆向思惟顯示五蘊決定是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若未來行先所未有定非有者，是即應非先無而有，如是應非無常決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　假設未來「沒有五蘊諸行」這件事，是常住不變的，則未來「沒有五蘊」來到現在，也決定不會有，如是現在五蘊不可能生起，則應當不是如前所說的「先無而有」，就不能說五蘊決定是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、正成</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科正成，以正面的思惟成立諸行決定無常。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由彼先時施設非有，非有為先，後時方有，是故未來諸行無常決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於未來，是觀待現在而有，是假施設有，因此未來並無「五蘊諸行」；既然未來「沒有五蘊諸行」，而來到現在才有「五蘊諸行」，因此未來「沒有五蘊諸行」這件事決定是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、先有而無2　午一、反顯</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科先有而無，五蘊現在有而過去沒有，分二科；第一科反顯，由施設過去「常」有過失，反顯過去諸行決定「無常」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若現在行從緣生已決定有者，是即應非先有而無，未來諸行便應非是無常決定，現在諸行亦應不與起盡相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段話意指，從眾緣所生的五蘊諸行若決定是有、是常的，就不可能「先有而無」，及「先無而有」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果現在的諸行從眾緣生已，決定是有、是常的，就不可能從現在走向過去，不可能從現在向於滅盡，即：現在不會成為過去，不會「先有而無」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若過去與現在是如此，則未來與現在也應相同：如果現在的五蘊諸行不是「先有而無」，則前文所說未來諸行便應該不是「先無而有」，因為不是決定無常，所以現在的五蘊諸行也不應有「起」（先無而有），及「盡」（先有而無）的生滅相了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、正成</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科正成，正面的思惟過去諸行決定「無常」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由現在行從緣生已，非決定有，以有為先，施設非有，是故過去諸行無常決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於現在的五蘊從眾緣所生起以後，並非決定永遠是有的，而是無常的；以現在五蘊諸行（有）剎那生滅為先，走向過去，向於滅盡，施設「非有」，因此過去五蘊諸行決定是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、起盡相應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科起盡相應，是約現在五蘊起盡相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是現在諸行，因未來行先無而有，因過去行先有而無，由此施設起盡相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是現在五蘊諸行，從未來「無」來到現在生起而「有」，又從現在「有」走向過去滅盡而「無」，由此施設現在五蘊諸行是起盡相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰五、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6441"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是故說言：當知去來諸行無常性尚決定，何況現在。是名諸行無常決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此說：當知過去、未來的諸行體性尚且決定都是無常的，更何況是現在的五蘊諸行呢？因為現在是觀待過去、未來而安立的，因此名為三世諸行無常決定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、苦性決定2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科苦性決定，說明五蘊諸行決定是苦，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何諸行苦性決定？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼五蘊諸行，決定是苦？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋4　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分四科；第一科標，總標出五蘊諸行決定是苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂去來諸行尚是生等苦法，何況現在。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過去五蘊有生老病死等苦，假如來生還有五蘊，也一樣是生老病死、愛別離苦，何況是現在五蘊，更是三苦、八苦、無量苦，眾苦聚集，難可免離。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">過去諸行是已度苦，未來諸行是未至苦，現在諸行是現前苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過去的五蘊諸行是已經度過了的苦，未來的五蘊諸行的苦還沒有來，而現在的五蘊諸行是現前的苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名諸行苦性決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過去有三苦、八苦、無量苦，未來、現在也一定是苦，所以諸行決定是苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、空性決定2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科空性決定，說明為何五蘊諸行是空性決定，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何諸行空性決定？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼諸行一定是空性？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6442"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋4　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分四科；第一科標，總標出諸行決定是空性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂去來諸行尚定空性，何況現在。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在過去、未來的五蘊諸行中都沒有我，尚且決定是空性，何況現在呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未來諸行其性未有，由此故空；過去諸行其性已滅，由此故空；現在諸行雖有未滅，諦義、勝義性所遠離，由此故空。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　未來諸行的體性還沒有出現，約不存在說空，由於未來諸行還沒有生起，因此未來的五蘊是空的；過去的諸行已經滅了，找不到過去的五蘊了，所以說是空。而現在諸行，感覺現在有，現在還存在，還沒有消失，但就聖者所證的真實性或勝義性的第一義諦來看，現在的五蘊也是不可得的，因為現在是觀待過去及未來而安立的，過去不可得，未來不可得，當然現在也不可得，所以現在也是空的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名諸行空性決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由這樣說五蘊諸行決定是空性的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》諦義勝義性所遠離者：謂現在行，相雖可得，非性實有。如幻化事雖現可見，非真實故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在五蘊諸行的相貌感覺好像存在，但它的體性並非實有。如同魔術師幻化出來的馬、兔等，現在雖然可以看到，但並不真實。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、無我決定2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無我決定，說明五蘊諸行是決定無我的，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何諸行無我決定？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼一切有為諸法是無我的，決定是如此呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6443"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋4　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分四科；第一科標，標出決定無我。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂去來諸行尚定無我，何況現在。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　過去、未來的五蘊諸行，一定是沒有「我」的；「我」的定義是恆常住不變、有主宰性、自主性的，但是過去、未來的有為法自己並無法作主，更何況是現在的有為法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未來諸行非我之相，未現前故；過去諸行非我之相，已越度故；現在諸行非我之相，正現前故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　未來諸行，還沒有現前，所謂的「我」在哪裡呢? 所以是無我相；過去諸行，已經過去了，見不到有「我」的停留，所以也是無我相；現在諸行，雖正現在前，但剎那就沒有了，是剎那剎那遷流不息的，找不到一個恆常住不變異的「我」的存在，所以也是無我相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無論是過去、現在或未來的諸行都是無我、無有主宰性的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名諸行無我決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由上文可知，是故三世五蘊諸行決定是無我的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》現在諸行等者：現在諸行，相雖可得，而非是我，唯彼行相正現前故。由是道理，無我決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　現在的諸行，雖然可以得到它的相貌，但剎那就又流逝了，非是一個恆常住、有主宰性的實我，只有它的行相剎那短暫的正現在眼前，由此道理，無我也是決定的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是由過去、現在、未來三相來思惟諸行無常、苦、空、無我。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、由二相4　寅一、無常決定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由二相，由二種相知道諸行決定是無常、苦、空、無我的，分四科；第一科無常決定，說明諸行決定是無常的二種相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由二相，當知諸行決定無常。一、由過去世已滅壞故；二、由未來、現在世是應滅壞法故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由二相，應當知道諸行決定是無常的：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由於過去的諸行已經消滅破壞，不存在了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由於未來、現在諸行是應當會滅壞的；過去已滅壞，雖然現在還沒有壞，但是將來一定會壞；未來也是一樣，未來如果有五蘊諸行，也一定是要滅壞，所以也可以由此二相來思惟無常。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6444"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、苦決定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科苦決定，說明諸行決定是苦的二種相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由二相，當知諸行決定是苦。一、是生等苦法故；二、是三苦性故。此諸苦相，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由二相了知五蘊諸行決定是苦的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、約八苦思惟，五蘊一定是苦的。五蘊有生、老、病、死苦、愛別離苦、怨憎會苦、求不得苦、五蘊熾盛苦；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、約三苦思惟，苦苦、壞苦、行苦，此中諸多苦惱的相貌，如前所說，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不論是八苦還是三苦，完全涵蓋了一切諸行，所以一切有為法皆苦是決定的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此諸苦相如前應知者：生等諸苦各由五相，如有尋有伺地決擇中說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/61.htm#65037:49117">陵本六十一卷十四頁4933</a>）又佛世尊說三苦性，所謂苦苦、壞苦、行苦，已如前知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生老病死、愛別離苦、怨憎會苦、求不得苦、五蘊熾盛苦各有五相（陵本六十一卷十四頁4933），這是約八苦來說，如〈決擇‧有尋有伺地〉卷61，1998頁中所說應該知道。又佛世尊說三苦性，所謂苦苦、壞苦、行苦，已如〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷34所說，應該能夠了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、空決定2　卯一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科空決定，說明諸行決定是空的二種相，分二科；第一科標列，標列出二相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由二相，當知諸行決定是空。一、畢竟離性空故；二、後方離性空故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由二種相貌，可以了知一切有為法決定是空的：一是畢竟離性空，二是後方（將來）離性空。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、隨釋2　辰一、畢竟離性空</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分二科；第一科畢竟離性空，說明畢竟離性空。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">畢竟離性空者，謂諸行中，我、我所性畢竟空故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　畢竟離性空方面，觀察在一切有為諸行當中並沒有恆常住、不變異、有主宰性的「我」的存在，也沒有我的相用，我、我所的體性都是畢竟空的，究竟是空，體相皆無，這是畢竟離性空。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、後方離性空</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後方離性空，說明後方離性空。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">後方離性空者，謂於已斷一切煩惱心解脫中，一切煩惱皆悉空故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　後方離性空方面，這是約成就聖道的阿羅漢已斷一切煩惱的心解脫中，所有煩惱皆悉淨空了的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　畢竟離性空是約自性清淨涅槃來說，因為本來就是無我、無我所，所以諸行決定是空；後方離性空，是約有餘依、無餘依涅槃來說，因為這時已斷一切煩惱，心得解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6445"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、無我決定</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無我決定，說明諸行決定是無我的二種相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由二相，當知諸行決定無我。一、諸行種種外性故；二、諸行從眾緣生，不自在故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由二相，應當知道五蘊決定是無我、無我所的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、約觀察五蘊無我、無我所，離開諸行以外並沒有常恆住不變異的「我」的實體存在，所以「離蘊無我」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、五蘊本身是從眾緣所生，不能自在，無有主宰性，不能自在就是無我，所以「即蘊無我」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又由二相當知諸行決定無我者：此中義顯，離蘊、即蘊計我都不可得，如次配釋二相應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是思惟諸行離蘊無我，即蘊也是無我的；離諸行之外找不到一個我，生命的現象只是因緣合和的五蘊在生住異滅，諸行本身當然也不是我，因為它是受制於因緣的，無有主宰性，這是由離蘊無我、即蘊無我，次第配合解釋二相來思惟，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、由十相</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由十相，由〈聲聞地〉所說的十相作分別，說明諸行決定是無常、苦、空、無我的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復由十相，當知諸行四相決定。謂由敗壞、變易、別離、相應、法性相故，非可樂、不安隱、相應、遠離、異相相故。如是等相，如前聲聞地已廣分別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由十種相，應當知道諸行無常、苦、空、無我，四相是決定的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、無常相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1、敗壞相：諸行決定會滅壞的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2、變易相：諸行決定是剎那剎那變化的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3、別離相：別離無常，任何可愛的內外諸行都不可能久住，必定要分離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4、相應相：是合會行（合會無常），因緣際會也是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　5、法性相：諸行的法性必定是無常的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、苦相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　6、非可樂相，指不可愛的苦苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　7、不安穩相，是指行苦，行苦是不安穩的，將來還是會遇到苦苦及壞苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　8、相應相，即是結縛行，也就是壞苦，樂受的時候通常會有貪煩惱與它相應，所以名相應相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、空相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　9. 遠離相，即是無所得行，也就是空行，行者觀察，在五蘊當中並沒有住著一個我，或是有情，沒有我、人、眾生、壽者，沒有這些有情所執著的，有主宰性、常恆住、不變異的我，這樣觀察名為由無所得行趣入空行。這時行者的心與空行相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、無我相：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　10. 異相相，諸行裡面並沒有我，是不自在的，與我的相貌是不一樣的，是即蘊無我。「我」的定義本來是常、一、有主宰性的，但是五蘊不是常住不變的，是眾緣和合，因此也不是有主宰性的，所以與「我」是異相，也就是由不自在行趣入無我行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遠離相是由無所得行，在諸行內外找不到我，是約體來說空。異相相則是約作用來說無我。前面〈聲聞地〉用這十相，來詳細分別思惟無常、苦、空、無我四相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6446"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》復由十相等者：聲聞地說：由十種行觀察苦諦，能隨悟入苦諦四行。何等為十？一、變異行，二、滅壞行，三、別離行，四、法性行，五、合會行，六、結縛行，七、不可愛行，八、不安隱行，九、無所得行，十、不自在行。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/34.htm#65051:27441">陵本三十四卷一頁2734</a>）今依彼義，隨應當知。謂此敗壞即是滅壞無常，變易即是變異無常，別離即是別離無常，相應即是合會無常，法性即是法性無常，非可樂即是不可愛苦，不安隱即是不安隱苦，相應即是結縛苦，遠離即是無所得空，異相即是不自在無我，由是故說諸行四相決定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈聲聞地〉說：由十相來觀察苦諦，能隨順悟入苦諦的無常、苦、空、無我四行。是哪十相？包括：變異行、滅壞行、別離行、法性行、合會行、結縛行、不可愛行、不安隱行、無所得行、不自在行。於〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷34，1089～1103頁已經提過，這裡依止那裡所說，隨所相應的應可了知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處文中所說的無常，其中敗壞相即是滅壞無常，變易相即是變異無常，別離相即是別離無常，相應相即是合會無常，法性相即是法性無常，非可樂相即是不可愛苦，不安隱相即是不安隱苦，相應相即是結縛苦，是樂受的相應行，遠離相即是無所得空，異相相即是不自在無我，因此說諸行四相決定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若要思惟無常、苦、空、無我，可以由三相來思惟，也可以由二相來思惟，也可以由〈聲聞地〉的十相來思惟，依自己所相應的來思惟，可以成就毗鉢舍那的觀慧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是本論說明「行擇攝」第一個別頌（界攝）中，第二句「愚相無常等定界」的「無常等定」，</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在《雜阿含經》中，相對應的經文為「陰相應」的第11至14經，如下標楷體所示：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第10頁：陰相應第11經；累計經數11經；大正藏（8）經<br />
　如是我聞：一時，佛住舍衛國祇樹給孤獨園。爾時、世尊告諸比丘：「過去、未來色無常，況現在色！聖弟子如是觀者，不顧過去色，不欣未來色，於現在色厭、離欲、正向滅盡。如是過去、未來受、想、行、識無常，況現在（受、想、行、）識！聖弟子如是觀者，不顧過去識，不欣未來識，於現在識厭、離欲、正向滅盡」。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第11至14經事實上是一樣的體裁。於第11經中，佛告訴比丘們，過去的色是無常的，未來的色也是無常的，何況是現在的色？由此可知，現在的五蘊必定也是剎那無常的，聖弟子們如果能夠這樣的觀察，不憶想過去年輕時的情景，因為那些都已無常滅壞，再也拿不回來了；也不要妄想未來要多健康、多強壯，未來尚未到來，怎知道能否如預期般到來。對於現在的色蘊也要厭離，不要有欲貪，應該要離欲，趣向於涅槃；同理，過去、未來的受、想、行、識也是無常的，何況現在的受、想、行、識，道理也是一樣，應對五蘊這樣觀察――不顧念過去的五蘊，不欣樂未來的五蘊，對現在的五蘊也應厭離，以成就初果的聖人可以達到的厭離五蘊的程度，乃至修道位聖人修得離欲的境界，最後證得正向滅盡的阿羅漢果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　而除了第11經之外，此段論文相應的還有第12至14經，如下標楷體所示：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="bb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:8px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><strong><span style="font-family:DFKai-SB">《雜上》第11頁：陰相應第12〜14經；累計經數12〜14經<br />
　如無常，（如是）苦，空，非我，亦復如是。時諸比丘聞佛所說，歡喜奉行。</span></strong></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如11經所提到的，無常是這樣的觀行方法，12至14經所說修苦、空、非我，也是一樣的觀法。從第11乃至第14經，都是佛開示無常、苦、空、無我真理的經典。行者應該加以研讀、理解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸八、界3　子一、辨品類2　丑一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科界，說明「行擇攝」第一個別頌（界攝）中，第二句「愚相無常等定界」的「界」，分三科；第一科辨品類，說明界的種類，又分二科；第一科標列，標示列出五種界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="66423:65053"></a>復次，依出世道作意修中，有五離繫品界。一者、斷界，二者、無欲界，三者、滅界，四者、有餘依涅槃界，五者、無餘依涅槃界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，彌勒菩薩又開示，依止修習出世間道的七作意當中，對於四聖諦──無常、苦、空、無我的十六行相作意思惟觀察，有五種遠離煩惱繫縛的品類，一、斷界，二、無欲界，三、滅界，四、有餘依涅槃界，五、無餘依涅槃界。於下文會一一詳細解說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、隨釋2　寅一、初二界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋這五種品類，分二科；第一科初二界，先解釋斷界和無欲界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="66168:65055"></a>謂見道所斷諸行斷故，名為斷界。修道所斷諸行斷故，名無欲界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見道位聖人見到諸法實相，將分別起的愛見煩惱全部斷除，證入初果，名為斷界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　初果聖人進入修道位，斷除欲界的煩惱，名無欲界。這是指三果聖者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、後三界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後三界，解釋滅界、有餘依涅槃界、無餘依涅槃界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此唯有餘依故，名有餘依涅槃界。此依滅故，名為滅界，亦名無餘依涅槃界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　阿羅漢將三界的愛見煩惱完全斷除，現生只剩下過去生有漏業所感得的果報，煩惱都不會再現行，名為有餘依涅槃界。到了臨終壽盡時，阿羅漢所依止的身體也滅了，身心都不可得，這是滅界，也名為無餘依涅槃界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、出異名6　丑一、諸行止</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科出異名，上面所說的五種離繫界又有不同的名稱，分六科；第一科諸行止，因斷除了分別起或俱生起的煩惱，名諸行止。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6447"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此五界，由一切行永寂靜故，名諸行止。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五種聖人的離繫界，於斷界，將三界分別起的愛見煩惱全部斷除，三惡道的五蘊諸行永遠寂靜；於無欲界，斷除欲界的欲貪煩惱，欲界的五蘊諸行永遠寂靜；於滅界及有餘依涅槃界，將三界的愛見煩惱完全斷除，當來三界所有五蘊諸行種子及現行永遠寂靜；於無餘依涅槃界，連今生所有五蘊諸行也永遠寂靜，不再有任何五蘊諸行，一切諸行徹底、究竟寂靜，是名諸行止。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是五界諸行止的漸次差別。因此五種離繫界也名為諸行止</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、空</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科空，說明五種離繫界亦名為空。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="63938:65062"></a>由我、我所、我慢、執著及與隨眠皆遠離故，說名為空。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五種聖人的離繫界，於斷界，將三界分別起的愛見煩惱全部斷除，分別起的我、我所、我慢、執著皆悉遠離；於無欲界，欲界的我、我所、我慢、執著及與隨眠皆悉遠離；於滅界及有餘依涅槃界，將分別起及俱生起的我、我所、我慢、執著及我慢煩惱的種子皆悉遠離；於無餘依涅槃界，不再有任何五蘊諸行，一切諸行徹底、究竟寂靜，我、我所、我慢、執著及我慢煩惱的種子畢竟不現行，說名為空。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是五種離繫界聖人所證的「空」的淺深差別，是故五種離繫界亦名為空。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由我我所等者：此中我、我所行，謂薩迦耶見。言我慢者，謂即此慢。即彼諸纏，名為執著。即彼麤重，名為隨眠。如攝異門分說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/83.htm#65063:63744">陵本八十三卷十八頁6332</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的我、我所行，是指薩迦耶見。所說的我慢，是我見所引起的慢。我、我所及我慢的煩惱現行名為執著；而我、我所行及我慢的煩惱種子也稱作隨眠。如〈攝異門分〉卷83，2505頁所說，應能了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、無所得</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無所得，五種離繫界亦名無所得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由一切相皆遠離故，名無所得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聖人因證得無分別智，遠離名想概念等虛妄分別，內心不再取著諸相，也名無所得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、愛盡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科愛盡，斷界亦名愛盡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="15167:65067"></a>於斷界中，一切隨順有漏法上所有貪愛皆遠離故，名為愛盡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　指初果聖人的境界，在斷界中，於一切隨順所有煩惱流漏法上即可愛的色乃至法等，因分別起的貪愛都遠離了，名為愛盡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、無欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科無欲，無欲界亦名無欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於無欲界所有欲貪皆遠離故，名為無欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三果以上的聖人將欲界的欲貪種子都斷除了，名為無欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑六、滅及涅槃</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科滅及涅槃，後三界亦名滅及涅槃。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6448"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於滅界中，及於有餘依、無餘依涅槃界中，如其所應皆永滅故、皆寂靜故，隨其次第，說名為滅，亦名涅槃。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在滅界，以及有餘依、無餘依涅槃界當中，於其所相應的三界分別及俱生的煩惱及當來的惑業苦皆永滅、寂靜，隨其次第，名為滅，也名為涅槃。因此滅是說明將先前所餘的煩惱都滅除證得阿羅漢果，於有餘依涅槃時內心寂靜，但還有果報之身，於無餘依涅槃時身心永滅。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上由不同角度來說明五界，因此還有六種不同的名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、明修習3　丑一、修厭</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科明修習，說明如何修厭、修離欲、修滅以成就五種離繫界，分三科；第一科修厭，修習厭離。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="16427:65074"></a>又於斷界未得為得勤修習故，名於諸行修厭。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又在斷界尚未成就，還沒有證得初果之前，行者要精勤不斷的修習止觀，厭離五蘊，名為於諸行修厭。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、修離欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科修離欲，修習離欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於無欲界未得為得勤修習故，名於諸行修離欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者尚未證得無欲界，因此還要精勤地修習離欲的止觀，斷除修所斷、應對治的欲貪，名於諸行修離欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、修滅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科修滅，修習滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於滅界未得為得勤修習故，名於諸行修滅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者尚未證滅界，於斷除煩惱的過程中還要不斷精勤修習止觀，斷除俱生起的煩惱種子成就滅界，名於諸行修滅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸九、二種漸次2　子一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科二種漸次，說明「行擇攝」第一個別頌（界攝）中，第三句「二種漸次應當知」的「二種漸次」，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，為心解脫勤修習者，有二種漸次。一、智漸次，二、智果漸次。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，為了使令心能解脫種種煩惱，精進修習止觀的行者，有二種次第：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、智慧漸次：說明行者要怎麼建立聞思修慧的次第，使令心得到解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、智果漸次：說明修行因智慧得到成果的漸次。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、隨釋2　丑一、智漸次3　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分二科；第一科智漸次，智慧增長的次第，又分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何智漸次？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是智慧增長的次第？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、無常故苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科無常故苦，解釋無常故苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6449"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂於諸行中，先起無常智，由思擇彼生滅道理故；次後於彼生相應行，觀為生法、老法，乃至憂苦熱惱等法；由是因緣，一切皆苦。此即依先無常智，生後苦智。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修行人透過聞慧，內心先學習生起無常智慧，知道五蘊是無常的，可以由三相、二相或十相來思惟無常。這樣思惟簡擇五蘊生滅的道理之後；其次再觀察五蘊相應生起時，會有生法、老法，乃至憂悲苦惱愁歎。依於這樣的思惟觀察，行者能體察到五蘊諸行生起是不斷變化的，乃至產生諸多憂悲愁歎苦惱，因而從無常轉為通達一切行都是苦。這是先依止無常智，由觀無常，然後生起苦智慧的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》乃至憂苦熱惱等法者：略無死法，說乃至言。略無愁歎，故置等言。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上面所說的生相應行不包括死法在裡面，因此說「乃至」這句話，思惟滅時才是思惟死法，又說憂苦熱惱等法，省略沒有說愁歎，因此安置「等」字。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、苦故無我</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科苦故無我，解釋苦故無我。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又彼諸行，由是生法乃至是熱惱法故，即是死生緣起展轉流轉不得自在行相道理，故無有我。此即依先苦智，生後無我智。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者再觀察色受想行識是生法乃至是熱惱法，僅是死了又生，生了又死，生生死死的緣起，由這樣死生緣起展轉流轉的行相，蘊涵無我的道理，顯示於眾緣所生的五蘊諸行，繫屬因緣，不能隨自己所期待的永遠健康快樂等，其中並沒有一個常恆住、有主宰性的我體或我的作用存在，因此是無我的。這就是依止苦智，然後生起無我智的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是觀無常故苦，苦故無我，是名智漸次。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　從聞慧開始，先觀無常生滅道理，生起無常智；由觀五蘊無常而生起苦智；再由觀察諸行皆苦，無有主宰性與自在性，進而生起無我的智慧。以上是名為智慧生起的漸次。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、智果漸次2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科智果漸次，說明修行成果的次第，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何智果漸次？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是智果的漸次呢？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、明漸次3　辰一、列四種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科明漸次，說明次第，又分三科；第一科列四種，列舉出有四種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂厭、離欲、解脫、遍解脫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　智果的漸次有厭、離欲、解脫、遍解脫這四種層次。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6450"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨別釋2　巳一、厭離欲解脫2　午一、第一差別2　未一、釋3　申一、厭</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨別釋，隨著各別解釋四種層次，分二科；第一科厭離欲解脫，解釋厭、離欲、解脫的體相，又分二科；第一科第一差別，解釋第一種差別義，又分二科；第一科釋，解釋，又分三科；第一科厭，解釋厭的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="72451:65097"></a><a name="53186:65097"></a><a name="40408:65097"></a><a name="16289:65097"></a>云何厭？謂有對治現前故，起厭逆想，令諸煩惱不復現行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者如何達到厭離色受想行識呢？如果有欲貪生起，應使令對治道現前，譬如修不淨觀，便能使心生起厭逆想，或是修其他如無常觀、苦觀、空觀，乃至無我觀等對治道。但是生起厭逆想時，只是伏煩惱現行，還未斷煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、離欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科離欲，解釋離欲的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何離欲？謂由修習厭心故，雖於對治不作意思惟，然於一切染愛事境貪不現行，此由伏斷增上力故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎樣是達到離欲的程度呢？由於常常修習厭離心，已經達到有思擇力的程度，因此雖然並無特別作意思惟對治道，然而即使觸對一切染愛的色聲香味觸境界，貪心也不會現行，這是由於伏斷煩惱的力量已經增強的緣故，這是約現行來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、解脫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科解脫，解釋解脫的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何解脫？謂即於此伏斷對治多修習故，永拔隨眠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎樣是達到解脫的程度呢？行者繼續思惟觀察諸行無常、苦、空、無我，先將煩惱現行數數的伏斷，久了伏斷煩惱的力量強大，這時有無漏修慧相應，將煩惱的種子斷除才得到解脫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上伏斷煩惱可以由淺到深，作這樣層次的解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名厭、離欲、解脫第一差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說即是厭、離欲、解脫的第一種解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、第二差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二差別，說明第二種差別義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。謂於厭位斷界極成滿，故名厭。即依止厭，除非想非非想處，於餘下地得離欲時，施設離欲位，故名離欲。於非想非非想處得離欲時，施設解脫位，故名解脫。是名厭、離欲、解脫第二差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有第二種不同的解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「厭」指證得初果。〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷13說：見道所斷諸行斷故；名為斷界。見道位時厭離五蘊的程度已達最極成滿，因初果聖人斷了分別起的煩惱種子，所以當觸對境界時，分別起的煩惱將不再現前，故名厭。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「離欲」指三果乃至四果向的有學聖人，初果已證得「厭」了，三果以上的聖人依止厭離心，觀無常、苦、空、無我所生起的厭離想，除了非想非非想處之外，其餘「下地」的無所有處、識無邊處、空無邊處、四禪、三禪、二禪、初禪，乃至將欲界的諸欲都斷除時，施設「離欲位」，所以名離欲。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在修道位來說，二果及初果三家家、二家家也已分斷部分的欲，如果將標準放寬廣一點也可以安立在離欲的地方。但通常離欲是從三果以上算起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「解脫」則指不僅將欲界、色界的煩惱都斷除，對於四空定、非想非非想處甚深禪定的愛著也都斷除，證得四果阿羅漢，才施設「解脫位」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是第二種解釋，厭、離欲、解脫的差別：「厭」指初果，「離欲」指三果和四果向，除了非想非非想處以外，其它下地的欲都遠離了。「解脫」則指四果阿羅漢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6451"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、遍解脫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科遍解脫，解釋遍解脫的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何遍解脫？謂由如是煩惱雜染解脫故，生等諸苦雜染亦普解脫，是名遍解脫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是遍解脫？由於行者解脫三界煩惱雜染，將來生老病死等諸苦的雜染也普遍解脫了，這時是名遍解脫。阿羅漢有二種：一是慧解脫阿羅漢，二是俱解脫阿羅漢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、結得名</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結得名，總結得名智果漸次。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="63078:65110"></a>如是由智增上力故，於諸行中起厭；由習厭故，得離欲；由習離欲故，得解脫及遍解脫。如是名為智果漸次。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者先有無常、苦、空、無我的聞慧，當這種智慧力量轉強增上至思慧、修慧時，依止禪定於定中修毗鉢舍那，觀察五蘊諸行，將依次得到這種智慧的結果：先生起「厭」；由於不斷的修習厭離心，就可離欲，觸對境界不生愛著；接著數數的修習離欲，將證得解脫，乃至來生的惑業苦都遍解脫了，這樣名為智果漸次。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、明所斷2　辰一、出邪執4　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明所斷，解釋智果漸次所斷除的煩惱，分二科；第一科出邪執，說明邪執的差別義，又分四科；第一科標，標出四種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中復有四種邪執。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在這當中有四種錯誤的執著，是應斷除的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為四？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪四種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、見邪執，二、慢邪執，三、自內邪執，四、他教邪執。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行者可能有這四種邪執：一、見邪執，二、慢邪執，三、自內邪執，四、他教邪執。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、釋2　午一、初二種2　未一、辨相2　申一、見邪執</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科初二種，說明初二種邪執的體相，又分二科；第一科辨相，辨明邪執的相狀，分二科；第一科見邪執，解釋見邪執的體相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="85p6452"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">見邪執者，謂於諸行中執我、我所。</span></strong></span></span></p>
